Means of Escape
He should have been back by now. Did he get lost in the woods?
The entrance is locked. Looks like you'll have to find another way out.
Seems there's a lake not too far away. Might be a good idea to check your map.
It's easy to get surrounded when facing many enemies, but the trick to avoiding this is to keep moving. This tactic may also lead you to useful items.
The lake can be accessed via the cliffside path beyond the windmill. Be sure to carefully look over the map so that you don't miss anything.
Things may get tough from here on out. Make sure you've got the weapons and upgrades you need before continuing on.
The target is being held inside the church on the hill. You've got the key, now all you have to do is get there.
You need a boat to cross the lake. If you look around the lakeside, you might be able to find one you can use.
You're as good as dead if the boat gets smashed up. Steer left and right to avoid obstacles.
Rescuing and keeping the target safe is your top priority, but you'll have to get the key to the church first.
The locations depicted in the mural have been marked on your map. Use them to aid your search.
You got what you need, but the lake's a big place. A treasure map can help you find any valuables you might have missed along the way.
The enemy becomes more aggressive at night. Make sure you're fully prepared before heading back to the church.
Despite the enemy's size, attacks to the face are effective. Consecutive attacks will cause its weak spot to appear on its back.
The target must be somewhere in the church. Best to explore every nook and cranny.
The enemy has swarmed around the church entrance. There's got to be another way out.
The enemy will try to forcibly carry Ashley away. Keep her out of harm's way by using suitable commands.
Keep moving to avoid being surrounded. Boarding up windows will also prevent enemies from getting in.
Protecting Ashley against large groups can be tricky. Maybe you can find a good place for her to hide while you deal with the threat.
Your weapons will do little to stop the big guy in black from pursuing Ashley.<lf>Your only hope is to run away.
Méndez's weak point is located on his back. It might be easier to target it from an elevated position.
Going back the way you came is no longer an option. Your only choice is to press forward and fight to keep Ashley safe.
The castle is heavily fortified. Find a way to take out the defenses.
The enemy down in the dungeons is sensitive to sound. Crouch to move more quietly while you search the area.
Numerous threats await you along the way to the courtyard. Stay vigilant to prevent Ashley from being taken.
After Ashley disappears into the courtyard alone, you'll have to make a large detour in order to reunite with her.
It's easy to lose your way in the middle of the castle. Make sure to check the map to find your bearings.
Living armor enemies are vulnerable to blue flames. Shine your lantern to immobilize them.
Flying enemies will swarm and attack from all directions. Lead them into a confined space to limit their movements.
Terrifying monsters skulk around in the water. Watch for the glow of their eyes right before they attack.
Ramón's right hand is vulnerable to the cold. Freezing it will make your attacks more effective.
Luis can take care of himself in a fight, so you don't need to protect him. Focus on the enemies that threaten you.
Stagger a giant while it's standing over the hatch in the center of the room to easily drop it into the blast furnace below.
Minecarts cannot be stopped once they've started moving. Shoot the track switches to change the cart's route and avoid danger.
This battle is best fought head-on with a knife. Try to parry your opponent's attacks and then aim to deal damage while he's still vulnerable.
Once you start your final assault on the castle, there's no going back. Look over the map and double-check that you haven't missed anything.
The zealots have a nasty surprise waiting for you in the clock tower. Proceed with caution.
Before settling the score with Ramón, make sure your equipment is up to snuff. Fully upgrade your weapons if you can afford it.
Ramón's true body is hidden inside the mouth of that huge monstrosity. Wait for an opening to attack it while doing your best to evade his attacks.
Krauser has taken Ashley. You've no choice but to go after them.
The soldiers use more deadly weapons. Be especially wary of those with rocket launchers.
These enemies will regenerate from normal attacks. It may be better to play it safe and run away until you can get your hands on the biosensor scope.
Ashley is being held captive, but she needs to be administered the suppressant before it's too late.
The equipment needed to remove the parasite is being kept in the cult's sanctuary at the top of the mountain.
With Ashley inside the crane, it's imperative that you protect it at all costs.
Make sure you've taken care of everything you need to before progressing further.
Krauser is quick and elusive. Keep your guard up and be especially careful when you lose sight of him.
Learn your opponent's attacks to know when to parry, dodge, or run away. And be careful not to get knocked off the ledge—the fall will kill you.
The helicopter will lay down a barrage of covering fire as you advance through the area, so try to draw the enemy out into the open.
The anti-aircraft gun is protected by armor on its sides. See if you can find a higher position to take aim at it from above.
Take control of a turret gun from the enemy for some heavy-duty firepower.
Luis's laboratory is in the sanctuary located at the top of the mountain. There, you'll find a way to eradicate the parasite.
The final battle against Saddler lies just up ahead. Take this last opportunity to prepare and upgrade your equipment.
Try to stay out of reach of Saddler's tentacles while you wait for an opening to attack. When that opening comes, stab at his vital points.
Time to make your escape, courtesy of Ada Wong.

Fall, 2004<lf>After the president's daughter is kidnapped, US agent Leon S. Kennedy follows eyewitness reports leading him to a small European village. With the weight of that fateful night in Raccoon City on his shoulders, he sets out on his mission.
Ashley Graham's trail has lead Leon straight into the belly of the beast. He's in pursuit, but one wrong move could spell his end.
"Your blood has accepted the Gift."<lf><lf>With these ominous words, Leon's formidable attacker vanished. While trying not to think about the true meaning behind them, Leon continues on in his search for Ashley.
After coughing up blood, Leon suddenly loses consciousness. Something is lingering inside his body, silently eroding him from inside out.<lf><lf>He needs to find Ashley...before it's too late...
Leon finally manages to locate Ashley and set her free, but his relief is cut short as a mob of villagers has the area surrounded. He must protect Ashley at all costs and escape the village.
Ashley discovers that she is also infected with the parasite known as the plaga. But all is not lost, as Luis offers them hope.<lf><lf>With no choice, Leon comforts her as they continue on.
Leon and Ashley evade their attackers and make their way to a castle. However, they have no idea of the evil that lies in wait behind its walls.
After using Leon's own knife against him, Ashley ran off deeper into the castle. Something wasn't right with her; it was as if she was being controlled like a puppet.<lf><lf>Confused and concerned, Leon goes after her.
Leon is finally reunited with Ashley, but he finds her paralyzed with guilt for what she has done. After some words of comfort, Ashley collects herself and the two set off together to meet up with Luis.
After Leon is caught in a trap, it was Ashley's turn to save the day. But their joyous reunion is short-lived as she is captured by the enemy once again.<lf><lf>Leon heads farther into the castle to rescue her.
Having fallen into Ramón's trap, Leon finds himself deep below the castle where he runs into Luis. Now they must work together to reach the surface and rescue Ashley.
Leon discovers that Jack Krauser, his former mentor, was involved in Ashley's kidnapping. Krauser ruthlessly murders Luis, then disappears without a trace. Confused and angry, Leon hurries to find Ashley and fulfill Luis's last wish.
Ada Wong shows up out of nowhere again, but Leon wonders where her allegiance truly lies. Is she an ally, or is she just using him again? Regardless of Ada's intentions, Leon can now pursue Krauser and save Ashley thanks to her.
Leon reunites with Ashley on an isolated island controlled by the cult, but they're running out of time. The plaga parasites within them continue to grow at a horrific rate.
Although finally able to lay his complicated history with Krauser to rest, Leon can't afford to waste time being sentimental now. Saddler has taken control of Ashley and disappeared into the depths of the island.
Fighting the parasite for control of his own body, Leon uses his last remaining strength to get Ashley to the lab in desperate hope that Luis's legacy can still save them.

About the Settings for Sending Play Data
If the customer has given consent, Capcom Co., Ltd. (the Company) will collect the personal information below that is related to gameplay in Biohazard RE:4 (the Game) and use that information for the purposes below.<lf><lf>About collected information:<lf>a. Information, such as your ID that is provided by us, your platform ID (user identification provided by a platform provider of games), and other information that identifies you as a player.<lf>b. Information related to the operation environment of our games, such as information about your computer, device, software, etc. <lf>c. Information of the country or region where you play our games and information related to your activities within our games.<lf>d. Log files and crash reports, and other similar information.  <lf>e. Content of your inquiry.<lf>f. Other information that we clearly specify prior to the collection of information.<lf><lf>Purpose of use:<lf>・For creation and use of statistical data for the analysis of play status of the Game. Capcom will use the statistical data for various purposes, including but not limited to improving or adding new features to the Game, future game development, and promotional activities (including disclosure of the statistical data) by Capcom.<lf>・For marketing purposes.<lf><lf>*Since we collect your Platform ID upon your playing of the Game, please acknowledge that in the event you play other Capcom games using the same Platform ID, your data collected upon playing the Game may be combined with your data collected upon playing other Capcom games and used for the purposes set forth herein.<lf><lf>Your data collected by Capcom will be sent and stored on the server in Japan, managed by Capcom and/or the server in Japan and/or U.S.A. of the cloud service providers contracted by Capcom, regardless of your country of residence.<lf>Your consent to data processing for purposes set forth herein is not mandatory, and you can freely decide whether or not to give your consent. Your game play will not be affected even if you choose not to consent.  <lf><lf>You may withdraw your consent at any time from the Options menu; however, this will not affect lawfulness of processing of the data collected prior to withdrawal of your consent.<lf><lf>Matters we have not explained so far about Capcom’s processing of your personal data are stated in our Capcom Games Privacy Policy (Console and PC games) (URL:https://www.capcom.co.jp/privacy/game/). Please be sure to read the Capcom Games Privacy Policy (Console and PC games) before giving us your consent.<lf><lf>Do you consent to data collection by the Company?

Blue Request Notes
You can take on tasks by collecting the Blue<lf>Request Notes posted around different areas.<lf><lf>View the requests you've taken in the Files menu.
Trading with the Merchant
Weapons and items can be bought or sold to<lf>the Merchant using Pesetas (ptas.). You can also<lf>upgrade or repair your weapons and equipment.
Merchant Requests
Once you've completed a task received from<lf>a Blue Request Note, you can claim the reward<lf>by talking to the Merchant.
Item Crafting
Certain materials such as resources, gunpowder,<lf>and knives can be used to craft different items.<lf><lf>The types of items that you can craft can be<lf>increased by obtaining new crafting recipes.
Captured Ashley
The enemy will try to grab Ashley and carry her<lf>off. If Leon is too far away when this occurs,<lf>they will get away, resulting in a game over.
Managing Your Items
If you cannot pick up an item because your<lf>inventory is full, you can try moving things<lf>around to make room via the Items menu.<lf><lf>You can also craft items to free up some space.
Knife Attacks
You can perform wide-sweeping slash attacks with <ICON SHOT>.<lf><lf>You can also deliver quick stab attacks with <ICON SHOT><lf>while holding <ICON PARRY>.
Ashley's Incapacitated State
Ashley will become temporarily incapacitated<lf>if she's attacked. She will die if she is attacked<lf>again while in this state.
Stealth Kills
If you sneak behind an enemy when you have<lf>a knife, you can take them out in a single move<lf>without making any noise.
Combining Treasures
You can view the treasures you've collected<lf>in the Key Items & Treasures menu.<lf><lf>Some treasures can be sold at a higher price<lf>by fitting them with gemstones.
Ashley Commands: Tight / Loose
Switch between Tight and Loose formation with <ICON NPC_INSTRUCTION>.<lf><lf>Ashley will stick close behind Leon while in<lf>Tight formation. This can be effective when<lf>running past enemies.
Switch between Tight and Loose formation with <ICON NPC_INSTRUCTION>.<lf><lf>Ashley will hang back behind Leon while in<lf>Loose formation. This can help her avoid<lf>enemy attacks.
Parrying
If you have a knife, you can parry an attack<lf>with <ICON PARRY> when the prompt appears in the<lf>bottom-right corner of the screen.<lf><lf>You can successfully parry even if you press<lf>it before the prompt appears. Time it right<lf>and the enemy will be staggered.
Charms
Charms can be swapped out via the Customize Case<lf>menu at any typewriter.
The Map
If you become lost, you can check your current<lf>position and objectives on the Map.<lf><lf>If you have a treasure map, you'll also be able<lf>to see the locations of hidden valuables.
Restoring Health
You can restore health using herbs or a first aid<lf>spray. The effects of herbs can be enhanced by<lf>combining them with other herbs.<lf><lf>Red herbs increase the amount of health recovered,<lf>while yellow herbs increase your maximum health.
Setting Weapon Shortcuts
You can set a weapon to a shortcut by selecting<lf>the weapon in the Items menu.<lf><lf>Up to eight weapons can be assigned at once:<lf>two weapons on each of the four directions.
Saving and Item Storage
You can save your progress at any typewriter.<lf><lf>You can also swap out weapons in your inventory<lf>via the Storage menu.
Used Key Items
Key items that no longer serve a purpose can<lf>be sold to the Merchant.
Melee Attacks
Melee attacks can be used on staggered enemies.<lf>If others are nearby, they will also be knocked<lf>back at the same time.<lf><lf>You can then deliver a fatal attack on the struck<lf>enemy with a knife, depending on their position.
Changing the Attaché Case
You can change your attaché case via the<lf>Customize Case menu at any typewriter.
Token Machines
You can use three silver or gold tokens at<lf>the token machine to win a random charm.<lf><lf>The more gold tokens you use, the greater<lf>your chances of getting a rare charm.
The biosensor scope can be used<lf>with any scope-compatible weapon.
Quick Turns
Perform a quick turn to quickly face in the<lf>opposite direction with <ICON QUICK_TURN_GUIDE>.<lf><lf>This action can also be turned off.
The quick turn action can be<lf>turned on in the Options menu.
Discounted Items
Discounts are only available during the chapters<lf>they appear in.

One of the few survivors of the Raccoon City Incident, he has continued to hone his skills as an agent for a secret US government program. His latest mission leads him to an isolated European village in his search for the president's missing daughter, Ashley Graham.
University student and beloved daughter of the US president. Currently missing. Her sudden disappearance was later determined to be a kidnapping, and the frantic search for her continues.
A person of interest that Leon encounters during his search for Ashley. Underneath his flippant personality lies some sort of ulterior motive.
An enigmatic woman whose fate seems to be connected to Leon's. She was presumed dead after the events of the Raccoon City Incident.
A mission coordinator belonging to the same government organization as Leon. Always professional and cool under pressure, she provides support to Leon via comms.
A weapons merchant that appears in various locations throughout the region. Although he is more than happy to sell and exchange goods with Leon, his true motives remain shrouded in mystery.
A large man whose towering physique seems to be impervious to damage from firearms. He is relentless in his pursuit of Ashley and his efforts to prevent Leon from saving her.
The twisted ruler of the region's castle. His fanatical adoration for his master results in a number of nightmarish schemes that spell horror for Leon and Ashley.
Leon's mentor from his days training as a new agent. Once a distinguished soldier, he is now in the employ of a heinous cult.
The leader of Los Iluminados. He wields an unearthly power, which allows him to control his countless disciples.
A plaza found in the center of the village. The monstrous locals that prowl the area do not take kindly to outsiders.
A modest church located on top of a small hill. Its purpose has been warped by the sinister teachings of a local cult, leaving it a shadow of its former self.
The residence of the Salazar family, its halls and dungeons now a reflection of the malevolent nature of the family's current patriarch—Ramón Salazar.
A large corridor that connects to the inner depths of the castle. The numerous artifacts that decorate the area depict the long and storied history of the Salazar family.
An island wharf fortified with strong defenses. Breaking through will prove to be a near-impossible task.
The island's stronghold is outfitted with an overwhelming amount of state-of-the-art defense systems. What lies on the far side must be of the utmost importance to them.

Chapter 1
Fall, 2004<lf>After the president's daughter is kidnapped, US agent<lf>Leon S. Kennedy follows eyewitness reports leading him to a<lf>small European village. With the weight of that fateful night<lf>in Raccoon City on his shoulders, he sets out on his mission.
Chapter 2
Ashley Graham's trail has lead Leon straight into the belly<lf>of the beast. He's in pursuit, but one wrong move could<lf>spell his end.
Chapter 3
"Your blood has accepted the Gift."<lf><lf>With these ominous words, Leon's formidable attacker<lf>vanished. While trying not to think about the true meaning<lf>behind them, Leon continues on in his search for Ashley.
Chapter 4
After coughing up blood, Leon suddenly loses consciousness.<lf>Something is lingering inside his body, silently eroding him<lf>from inside out.<lf><lf>He needs to find Ashley...before it's too late...
Chapter 5
Leon finally manages to locate Ashley and set her free,<lf>but his relief is cut short as a mob of villagers has<lf>the area surrounded.<lf><lf>He must protect Ashley at all costs and escape the village.
Chapter 6
Ashley discovers that she is also infected with the<lf>parasite known as the plaga. But all is not lost,<lf>as Luis offers them hope.<lf><lf>With no choice, Leon comforts her as they continue on.
Chapter 7
Leon and Ashley evade their attackers and make their<lf>way to a castle. However, they have no idea of the evil<lf>that lies in wait behind its walls.
Chapter 8
After using Leon's own knife against him, Ashley ran off<lf>deeper into the castle. Something wasn't right with her;<lf>it was as if she was being controlled like a puppet.<lf><lf>Confused and concerned, Leon goes after her.
Chapter 9
Leon is finally reunited with Ashley, but he finds<lf>her paralyzed with guilt for what she has done.<lf><lf>After some words of comfort, Ashley collects herself<lf>and the two set off together to meet up with Luis.
Chapter 10
After Leon is caught in a trap, it was Ashley's turn<lf>to save the day. But their joyous reunion is short-<lf>lived as she is captured by the enemy once again.<lf><lf>Leon heads farther into the castle to rescue her.
Chapter 11
Having fallen into Ramón's trap, Leon finds himself<lf>deep below the castle where he runs into Luis.<lf>Now they must work together to reach the surface<lf>and rescue Ashley.
Chapter 12
Leon discovers that Jack Krauser, his former mentor,<lf>was involved in Ashley's kidnapping. Krauser ruthlessly<lf>murders Luis, then disappears without a trace.<lf>Confused and angry, Leon hurries to find Ashley<lf>and fulfill Luis's last wish.
Chapter 13
Ada Wong shows up out of nowhere again, but Leon<lf>wonders where her allegiance truly lies. Is she an ally,<lf>or is she just using him again?<lf>Regardless of Ada's intentions, Leon can now pursue<lf>Krauser and save Ashley thanks to her.
Chapter 14
Leon reunites with Ashley on an isolated island<lf>controlled by the cult, but they're running out of time.<lf>The plaga parasites within them continue to grow<lf>at a horrific rate.
Chapter 15
Although finally able to lay his complicated history with<lf>Krauser to rest, Leon can't afford to waste time being<lf>sentimental now. Saddler has taken control of Ashley<lf>and disappeared into the depths of the island.
Chapter 16
Fighting the parasite for control of his own body, Leon uses<lf>his last remaining strength to get Ashley to the lab in<lf>desperate hope that Luis's legacy can still save them.
The blue papers that you find scattered around the area<lf>are Request Notes. By picking one up, you will accept<lf>a request. The details of accepted requests can be viewed<lf>in the Files menu.
Request Rewards
Once you've completed a request, head to the Merchant<lf>to receive spinels as a reward.
You can create various kinds of ammo by combining<lf>resources and gunpowder. Some knives can also be<lf>used as crafting materials.<lf>Obtaining new crafting recipes will increase the types<lf>of items and ammo that you can create.
Managing Items
If your attaché case is full, you can rearrange things in<lf>the Items menu to make room for more items.<lf>Using consumables or crafting items can also create<lf>more space in your inventory.
Attacking while your knife is readied will deliver<lf>quick forward thrusts.
Knife Escape
If you have a knife, you will be able to quickly escape<lf>from an enemy in most circumstances.<lf><lf>However, the knife's durability will be greatly reduced.
Some treasures can be sold at a higher price when fitted<lf>with certain gemstones.<lf><lf>View the treasures you've collected in the Key Items &<lf>Treasures menu.
Ashley Commands: Tight Formation
When commanded to move into Tight formation, Ashley<lf>will stick close to Leon at all times.<lf><lf>This formation is particularly useful when on the move<lf>or trying to evade enemies.
If you have a knife, some enemy attacks can be<lf>parried by performing the action just before the hit lands.<lf><lf>Time it right and the enemy will be staggered, giving you<lf>a chance to attack.
Ashley Commands: Loose Formation
When commanded to move into Loose formation,<lf>Ashley will hang back and distance herself from Leon.<lf><lf>In this formation, Ashley will protect herself by avoiding<lf>enemies and staying clear of combat.
The map isn't just for figuring out where you are.<lf>It's also great for seeing where your objectives are<lf>or locating unclaimed items.
Treasure maps will point out the locations of<lf>treasure on your map.
You can restore health using herbs or first aid sprays.<lf>You can also craft more effective recovery items by<lf>combining specific herbs in the Items menu.
You can set a weapon to a shortcut by selecting<lf>the weapon in the Items menu.<lf><lf>Up to eight weapons can be assigned at once.
You can temporarily deposit your equipment via<lf>the Storage menu at any typewriter.<lf><lf>Stash away things like bulky weapons to make<lf>space for other items in your attaché case.
Saving
When you see a typewriter, remember that saving is free,<lf>so save often and save a life.
Key items that no longer serve a purpose can be sold<lf>to the Merchant.
Melee attacks can be used on staggered enemies. If others<lf>are nearby, they will also be knocked back at the same time.<lf><lf>You can then deliver a fatal attack on the struck enemy<lf>with a knife, depending on their position.
Customizing Your Case
You can change your attaché case or swap out charms via<lf>the Customize Case menu at any typewriter.<lf><lf>Cases and charms each have their own special effects.
You can change the quick turn button or turn the action off<lf>in the Options menu.
When Aiming Weapons
Shooting a weapon while the reticle is zoomed in will<lf>increase the stagger and critical hit rate on enemies.
Crouching
Moving while in the crouched position can help you<lf>avoid enemy detection.
Upgrading Your Weapons
Most weapons can be upgraded by the Merchant.<lf>If you keep running into difficulty during combat,<lf>consider upgrading your weapons to give yourself<lf>some more firepower.
Repairing the Combat Knife
The combat knife can be repaired by the Merchant<lf>if it is broken. It can also be upgraded to increase<lf>its durability, making it harder to break.
Trading
Spinels can be traded in to the Merchant for special items.
Using Typewriters
You can't use typewriters while speaking through comms<lf>or when enemies are nearby.
Viewing Information
You can view the contents of documents and comms<lf>that you've received via the Files menu.<lf><lf>They may contain some important information.
Clockwork Castellans
If you ever hear the steady cadence of a wind-up doll,<lf>it means that there's a Clockwork Castellan nearby.<lf><lf>It might be a good idea to find and destroy it.
Scope Magnification
You can choose whether the level of scope<lf>magnification stays the same or resets after<lf>you stop aiming in the Options menu.
The higher you score, the more tokens you'll earn.<lf>Exchange them at a token machine to receive prizes.
Changing Difficulty
You can change the game's difficulty level from<lf>Standard to Assisted in the game over screen.
Incapacitated Ashley
Ashley will become temporarily incapacitated<lf>if she's attacked.<lf><lf>If attacked again in this state, she will die and<lf>the game will be over.
If Ashley is caught by the enemy and carried away,<lf>the game will be over.<lf><lf>Rescue her before the gauge in the bottom-right<lf>corner of the screen runs out.
Most enemy attacks can be parried, with some exceptions.<lf>Time a parry just right and the enemy will be staggered,<lf>giving you a chance to follow up with an attack.
Crouch Dodging
Some enemy attacks such as grapples and thrown weapons<lf>can be dodged by crouching.
Knife Kills
You can perform a fatal attack with a knife when you<lf>approach an enemy from behind or stagger them with<lf>something like a flash grenade.
Finishing Enemies Off
Some enemies will get back up even after you think they've<lf>been defeated. You can prevent this by performing a fatal<lf>attack on them with a knife while they are on the ground.
Shooting dynamite will cause it to explode.<lf>This also applies to the unlit sticks of dynamite<lf>held in the hands of certain enemies.
Red-robed Zealots
The chanting prayers of these foes strengthen<lf>other enemies surrounding them.
Throw Attacks
Approach a kneeling enemy from behind to perform<lf>a throw attack.
Plaga Weakness
The parasites that emerge out of the bodies of some<lf>enemies are vulnerable to intense light.<lf><lf>Using weapons that emit light can be very effective.
Knife Defense
Some attacks can be blocked with a knife.
Parasite's Mouth
You can deal a lot of damage to the large parasites<lf>that emerge out of some enemy's bodies by attacking<lf>their weak point—the mouth.
Attacks from Above
Pass below hanging enemies at your own risk.
Latching On
Some parasites can move around independently from the host<lf>and latch on to enemies, making them even more ferocious.<lf>Take them out before they can do this.
The Chainsaw Enemies
The villagers that wield chainsaws are formidable foes.<lf>Don't feel like you have to defeat them; sometimes it's<lf>just better to run away.
Sightless Enemies: Sound
Making noise alerts these enemies to your position, so tread<lf>carefully. Walking is quieter than running, and crouching<lf>is quieter than walking.
Sightless Enemies: Weakness
If you attack the exposed parasites on these enemies,<lf>you can cause a lot of damage.
Sightless Enemies: Friendly Fire
These enemies cannot see and are unable to differentiate<lf>between friend and foe. Use this to your advantage by<lf>trying to lure them into the path of another enemy.
Sightless Enemies: Weapons
Enemies that cannot see are more sensitive to sound.<lf>It is wise to use weapons that make less noise when nearby.
Sightless Enemies: Ringing Bells
You can draw the enemy's attention by shooting<lf>a bell to make a loud noise.
Living Armor: Blue Flames
These enemies cannot move when exposed to blue flames.
Living Armor: Armor
You won't get very far attacking the areas protected<lf>by the armor. Instead, aim for the scarcely visible<lf>parasite through the gaps.
Living Armor: Strong Attacks
The two-handed overhead sword attacks are a force to<lf>be reckoned with. Parrying them will greatly reduce<lf>your knife's durability.
Living Armor: Weakness
Exposed parasites are vulnerable to intense light.<lf>Using weapons that emit light can be very effective.
Living Armor: Explosive Weapons
Explosive weapons such as hand grenades are<lf>effective at damaging armored enemies.
Flying Enemies
Flying enemies have the advantage in large, open areas.<lf>Draw them into a confined space to limit their mobility.
Shooting Enemies: Rapid Attacks
Advance against enemies that launch rapid-fire attacks<lf>from a distance by taking cover as you move.
Shooting Enemies: Crossbows
Take advantage of the time it takes for these enemies<lf>to reload. Their magazines explode with light attacks.
Regenerating Enemies: Recovery
These enemies will continue to regenerate unless<lf>you destroy the parasites inside their bodies.
Regenerating Enemies: Weakness 1
Consecutive attacks will expose the parasites<lf>inside these enemies. Once exposed, you can<lf>attack and damage them directly.
Regenerating Enemies: Weakness 2
Weapons with high penetration power can also damage<lf>the unexposed parasites inside these enemies.
Regenerating Enemies: Biosensor Scope
Using a weapon with the biosensor scope mounted onto it<lf>will give you the ability to accurately target the parasites<lf>inside these enemies.
Regenerating Enemies: Mutation
Enemies with high-regenerative capabilities may transform<lf>and heal themselves when threatened.
Regenerating Enemies: Instant Death
Getting grabbed by high-regenerative enemies means<lf>certain death if you don't react quickly. Use a knife<lf>to escape as fast as possible.
Regenerating Enemies: Weak Point
When these enemies mutate, the parasites inside their<lf>bodies will move to their heads. Aim for their mouths<lf>to deal damage directly to them.
Lord of the Lake: Dodging
Running into an obstacle or being hit by an attack will<lf>damage your boat. It will then capsize if it receives<lf>too much damage.<lf><lf>Dodge obstacles and attacks by moving left or right.
Lord of the Lake: Harpoons
Harpoons that hit the water lose power.<lf><lf>When attacking, be sure to aim for the part of the enemy<lf>that's exposed above the surface.
Returning the Favor
An unexpected ally will pay you back for your<lf>kindness by drawing the giant's attention away.
Village Chief: Escape
Méndez won't be affected by any of your attacks.<lf>It's just better to run away.
Village Chief: Weakness
You can stagger Méndez by attacking the eye on his back.<lf>Getting a clear line of sight will help you hit your mark.
Village Chief: Follow-up Attacks
When Méndez is stunned, he is vulnerable<lf>to follow-up knife attacks.
Ramón's Assassin: Surprise Attacks
Don't let your guard down when the enemy disappears.<lf>Keep an eye on the ceiling, floor, and holes in the walls<lf>so you can avoid surprise attacks.
Ramón's Assassin: How to Attack
Shooting recklessly at this quick enemy will only waste<lf>ammunition. You must find an effective means of attack<lf>if you hope to survive.
Ramón's Assassin: Weakness
Exposing the enemy to liquid nitrogen will weaken<lf>it and slow it down.
Ramón's Assassin: Elevator
If the situation looks dire, get to the elevator and make<lf>your escape. You don't have to defeat the enemy, you just<lf>have to stay alive long enough for the elevator to arrive.
Armored Giant: Futile Attacks
Armored giants cannot be damaged by normal attacks.
Armored Giant: Roars
When you hear the giant's roar, take cover from<lf>the boulders it throws at you.
Armored Giant: Blast Furnace
To drop an enemy into the blast furnace, you'll need<lf>to find a way to get it to stay still over the hatch.
Krauser: Knife Fight
Krauser's attacks can be parried. Take full advantage<lf>of this by facing him head-on with a knife.
Krauser: Recovery Items
Use a recovery item when your health is low to stay alive.
Krauser: Finding Another Knife
Don't worry too much when your knife breaks.<lf>Stay calm and look around because you may<lf>find another.
Krauser: Deadly Falls
Trying to fight near the edge of a large drop<lf>is just an accident waiting to happen.
Ramón: Acid Spray
Use your surroundings to take cover and safely<lf>avoid Ramón's acid spray attacks.
Ramón: Attack Opportunity
Keep your eye out for the opening that immediately<lf>follows Ramón's acid spray attack and aim for his<lf>true form inside the mouth.
Ramón: Signs of a Big Attack
When Ramón suddenly stops moving overhead and begins<lf>to aim, it means that he's getting ready for his next big<lf>attack. This is also a good opportunity to aim for his vital<lf>points and get some damage in.
Ramón: Acid Bombs
Acid bombs dropped on the ground will explode when<lf>you get too close, but they can be destroyed by shooting<lf>them from a safe distance.
Ramón: Knife Attacks
If Ramón falls to the ground, you'll have a chance<lf>to perform a follow-up attack with a knife.
Krauser (Ruins): Bow
The arrows that Krauser shoots are fitted with explosives.<lf>Watch out for his laser sight to know where he's aiming<lf>and avoid his devastating attacks.
Krauser (Ruins): Laser Traps
The laser traps set up by Krauser cannot be<lf>deactivated, but they can be destroyed by<lf>safely shooting them from a distance.
Krauser (Ruins): Close Quarters
Krauser's knife attacks can be parried.
Krauser (Ruins): Fear of Heights
Krauser (Ruins): Jump Attacks
Evade Krauser's jump attacks by quickly moving<lf>out of the way.
Krauser (Ruins): Charge Attacks
Krauser's charge attacks with his mutated arm<lf>can be parried.
Saddler: Keeping Your Distance
Put enough distance between you and Saddler<lf>to stay out of reach of his tentacles.
Saddler: Vital Points
You can slow Saddler down by attacking<lf>the vital points on his mutated legs.
Mutated Saddler: Weakness
Aim for the tissue surrounding Saddler's body.
Moving While Crouching
Getting surrounded by a large number of enemies can<lf>be dangerous. Keep moving to avoid such situations.
Being Outnumbered
Sometimes, defeating all the enemies just isn't feasible.<lf>If a situation seems insurmountable, try running around<lf>until you find a way out.
Beware of Falling Rocks
Watch out for falling rocks. If they fall on top of you,<lf>you will die instantly.
Bear Traps
Bear traps can be disabled with an attack.
Using Knives Effectively
When it comes to close-quarter combat, a knife may be<lf>more effective than a gun. Being able to parry an enemy's<lf>attack will give you even more of an advantage.
Take Things Slow
Recklessly rushing into an area is a good way to get<lf>into trouble. Sometimes, it's more advantageous<lf>to take things slow and pick off threats one by one.
Using Your Surroundings
Laid traps work against enemies as well.<lf>Maybe you can use them to your advantage.
Advantageous Position
If you find yourself surrounded by quick enemies, try luring<lf>them into a narrow space to limit their movements.
Falling
Knocking an enemy off a ledge with a shotgun or<lf>melee attack will cause them to fall to their death.
Barricading the Windows
Use wooden planks to board up the windows and prevent<lf>the enemy from getting in.
Ashley can be instructed to hide inside lockers.
Catapults
You can disable a catapult by killing the enemy that<lf>is operating it.
Sun and Moon Shutters
Shutters and levers have matching symbols.<lf><lf>The symbol displayed on a lever indicates<lf>which shutter is currently open.
Track Switches
You can change the minecart's path by shooting<lf>the track switches.
Chainsaw Enemy
Keep an eye on the enemy with a chainsaw when<lf>he's riding parallel to your cart.
Iron Balls
Watch out for the rolling iron balls. Getting hit by<lf>one means instant death.
Lift Battle
The lift has a weight limit and will stop if exceeded.<lf>Try to defeat the enemies before they get on.
Unstable Surfaces
Running on an unstable surface may cause<lf>it to collapse under you.
Spotlights
Being detected by a spotlight will sound an alarm that will<lf>call enemy reinforcements.<lf><lf>This will also happen if an enemy is alerted to your presence.
The Crane
If the enemy breaks into the crane, they'll<lf>get Ashley and the game will be over.
The Anti-aircraft Gun
You can destroy the anti-aircraft gun using<lf>the turret gun at the top of the stronghold.
Take control of a turret gun from the enemy for some<lf>heavy-duty firepower.
Body Bags
The biosensor scope will allow you to see what's<lf>inside of bags.
Wire Traps
Wire traps can be detonated with an attack or by approaching<lf>them carefully and deactivating them.

Data Processing in Resident Evil Village<lf><lf>We, Capcom Co., Ltd. (“Capcom”), will collect and process your personal data according to our Privacy Policy upon your usage of Resident Evil Village (“Game”). <lf>Privacy Policy (https://www.capcom.co.jp/privacy/game/)<lf><lf>This Game also provides you a function to share your game-play data with the RESIDENT EVIL.NET service (“RE NET”) (https://www.residentevil.net) operated by Capcom. <lf><lf>RE NET is a free interlocking web service support the Resident Evil series, providing features which allows you to view various data such as;<lf>- world statistics based on enormous play data from players all over the world;<lf>- detailed play data; and<lf>- ranking <lf><lf>Your consent to share your gameplay data with the RE NET is optional, and you may freely decide whether to give your consent.  Your gameplay experience will not be affected by the denial of the consent.<lf><lf>Capcom will collect the following personal data with your consent for the following purposes:<lf><lf>Collected information:<lf>(a)  Identifying informationIdentification data provided by the platform providers;<lf>(b)  In-game setting information;<lf>(c)  Gameplay data (including region information); and,<lf>(d)  Logs of in-game communication on the network connection; and,<lf><lf>Purpose of use:<lf>- To enable you to use the services related to this Game on the RE NET website;<lf>- To better understand the Capcom’s users and utilize the findings for product development and marketing purposes of Capcom’s products; and,<lf>- To create statistical data for utilization and publication. <lf><lf><lf>In relation to the RE NET, your personal data will be sent and stored on the server in Japan, managed by Capcom and/or the server in Japan and/or U.S.A of the cloud service providers contracted by Capcom, regardless of your country of residence.<lf>If your data is transferred outside the European Economic Area (EEA) for storage and processing of the data, Capcom will comply with applicable data protection laws, including GDPR.<lf><lf>You may withdraw your consent at any time on “RE NET” from the “Options” screen which will not affect the legitimate process of the data transmitted to Capcom prior to the withdrawal of your consent, and such data will remain accessible on the RE NET website.<lf><lf>Please be noted that, in order to use the RE NET website, you need to consent to the RE NET Terms of Use as well as its Privacy Policy provided separately.  <lf><lf>Do you consent to share your gameplay data with RE NET?<lf><lf>Yes/No

Information, such as your ID that is provided by us, your platform ID (user identification provided by a platform provider of games), and other information that identifies you as a player.<lf>b. Information related to the operation environment of our games, such as information about your computer, device, software, etc. <lf>c. Information of the country or region where you play our games and information related to your activities within our games.<lf>d. Log files and crash reports, and other similar information.  <lf>e. Content of your inquiry.<lf>f. Other information that we clearly specify prior to the collection of information.<lf><lf>Purpose of use:<lf>・For creation and use of statistical data for the analysis of play status of the Game. Capcom will use the statistical data for various purposes, including but not limited to improving or adding new features to the Game, future game development, and promotional activities (including disclosure of the statistical data) by Capcom.<lf>・For marketing purposes.<lf><lf>*Since we collect your Platform ID upon your playing of the Game, please acknowledge that in the event you play other Capcom games using the same Platform ID, your data collected upon playing the Game may be combined with your data collected upon playing other Capcom games and used for the purposes set forth herein.<lf><lf>Your data collected by Capcom will be sent and stored on the server in Japan, managed by Capcom and/or the server in Japan and/or U.S.A. of the cloud service providers contracted by Capcom, regardless of your country of residence.<lf>Your consent to data processing for purposes set forth herein is not mandatory, and you can freely decide whether or not to give your consent. <COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Sys_RichTutorialTitle_Dummy
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Sys_RichTutorialBody_Dummy
Blue Request Notes
You can take on tasks by collecting the Blue<lf>Request Notes posted around different areas.<lf><lf>View the requests you've taken in the Files menu.
Trading with the Merchant
Weapons and items can be bought or sold to<lf>the Merchant using Pesetas (ptas.). You can also<lf>upgrade or repair your weapons and equipment.
Merchant Requests
Once you've completed a task received from<lf>a Blue Request Note, you can claim the reward<lf>by talking to the Merchant.
Item Crafting
Certain materials such as resources, gunpowder,<lf>and knives can be used to craft different items.<lf><lf>The types of items that you can craft can be<lf>increased by obtaining new crafting recipes.
Captured Ashley
The enemy will try to grab Ashley and carry her<lf>off. If Leon is too far away when this occurs,<lf>they will get away, resulting in a game over.
Managing Your Items
If you cannot pick up an item because your<lf>inventory is full, you can try moving things<lf>around to make room via the Items menu.<lf><lf>You can also craft items to free up some space.
Knife Attacks
You can perform wide-sweeping slash attacks with <ICON SHOT>.<lf><lf>You can also deliver quick stab attacks with <ICON SHOT><lf>while holding <ICON PARRY>.
Ashley's Incapacitated State
Ashley will become temporarily incapacitated<lf>if she's attacked. She will die if she is attacked<lf>again while in this state.
Stealth Kills
If you sneak behind an enemy when you have<lf>a knife, you can take them out in a single move<lf>without making any noise.
Combining Treasures
You can view the treasures you've collected<lf>in the Key Items & Treasures menu.<lf><lf>Some treasures can be sold at a higher price<lf>by fitting them with gemstones.
Ashley Commands: Tight / Loose
Switch between Tight and Loose formation with <ICON NPC_INSTRUCTION>.<lf><lf>Ashley will stick close behind Leon while in<lf>Tight formation. This can be effective when<lf>running past enemies.
Ashley Commands: Tight / Loose
Switch between Tight and Loose formation with <ICON NPC_INSTRUCTION>.<lf><lf>Ashley will hang back behind Leon while in<lf>Loose formation. This can help her avoid<lf>enemy attacks.
Parrying
If you have a knife, you can parry an attack<lf>with <ICON PARRY> when the prompt appears in the<lf>bottom-right corner of the screen.<lf><lf>You can successfully parry even if you press<lf>it before the prompt appears. Time it right<lf>and the enemy will be staggered.
Charms
Charms can be swapped out via the Customize Case<lf>menu at any typewriter.
The Map
If you become lost, you can check your current<lf>position and objectives on the Map.<lf><lf>If you have a treasure map, you'll also be able<lf>to see the locations of hidden valuables.
Restoring Health
You can restore health using herbs or a first aid<lf>spray. The effects of herbs can be enhanced by<lf>combining them with other herbs.<lf><lf>Red herbs increase the amount of health recovered,<lf>while yellow herbs increase your maximum health.
Setting Weapon Shortcuts
You can set a weapon to a shortcut by selecting<lf>the weapon in the Items menu.<lf><lf>Up to eight weapons can be assigned at once:<lf>two weapons on each of the four directions.
Saving and Item Storage
You can save your progress at any typewriter.<lf><lf>You can also swap out weapons in your inventory<lf>via the Storage menu.
Used Key Items
Key items that no longer serve a purpose can<lf>be sold to the Merchant.
Melee Attacks
Melee attacks can be used on staggered enemies.<lf>If others are nearby, they will also be knocked<lf>back at the same time.<lf><lf>You can then deliver a fatal attack on the struck<lf>enemy with a knife, depending on their position.
Changing the Attaché Case
You can change your attaché case via the<lf>Customize Case menu at any typewriter.
Token Machines
You can use three silver or gold tokens at<lf>the token machine to win a random charm.<lf><lf>The more gold tokens you use, the greater<lf>your chances of getting a rare charm.
Biosensor Scope
The biosensor scope can be used<lf>with any scope-compatible weapon.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Sys_RichTutorialTitle_022
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Sys_RichTutorialBody_022
Quick Turns
Perform a quick turn to quickly face in the<lf>opposite direction with <ICON QUICK_TURN_GUIDE>.<lf><lf>This action can also be turned off.
The quick turn action can be<lf>turned on in the Options menu.
Discounted Items
Discounts are only available during the chapters<lf>they appear in.

Chapter 1
Fall, 2004<lf>After the president's daughter is kidnapped, US agent<lf>Leon S. Kennedy follows eyewitness reports leading him to a<lf>small European village. With the weight of that fateful night<lf>in Raccoon City on his shoulders, he sets out on his mission.
Chapter 2
Ashley Graham's trail has lead Leon straight into the belly<lf>of the beast. He's in pursuit, but one wrong move could<lf>spell his end.
Chapter 3
Your blood has accepted the Gift.<lf><lf>With these ominous words, Leon's formidable attacker<lf>vanished. While trying not to think about the true meaning<lf>behind them, Leon continues on in his search for Ashley.
Chapter 4
After coughing up blood, Leon suddenly loses consciousness.<lf>Something is lingering inside his body, silently eroding him<lf>from inside out.<lf><lf>He needs to find Ashley...before it's too late...
Chapter 5
Leon finally manages to locate Ashley and set her free,<lf>but his relief is cut short as a mob of villagers has<lf>the area surrounded.<lf><lf>He must protect Ashley at all costs and escape the village.
Chapter 6
Ashley discovers that she is also infected with the<lf>parasite known as the plaga. But all is not lost,<lf>as Luis offers them hope.<lf><lf>With no choice, Leon comforts her as they continue on.
Chapter 7
Leon and Ashley evade their attackers and make their<lf>way to a castle. However, they have no idea of the evil<lf>that lies in wait behind its walls.
Chapter 8
After using Leon's own knife against him, Ashley ran off<lf>deeper into the castle. Something wasn't right with her;<lf>it was as if she was being controlled like a puppet.<lf><lf>Confused and concerned, Leon goes after her.
Chapter 9
Leon is finally reunited with Ashley, but he finds<lf>her paralyzed with guilt for what she has done.<lf><lf>After some words of comfort, Ashley collects herself<lf>and the two set off together to meet up with Luis.
Chapter 10
After Leon is caught in a trap, it was Ashley's turn<lf>to save the day. But their joyous reunion is short-<lf>lived as she is captured by the enemy once again.<lf><lf>Leon heads farther into the castle to rescue her.
Chapter 11
Having fallen into Ramón's trap, Leon finds himself<lf>deep below the castle where he runs into Luis.<lf>Now they must work together to reach the surface<lf>and rescue Ashley.
Chapter 12
Leon discovers that Jack Krauser, his former mentor,<lf>was involved in Ashley's kidnapping. Krauser ruthlessly<lf>murders Luis, then disappears without a trace.<lf>Confused and angry, Leon hurries to find Ashley<lf>and fulfill Luis's last wish.
Chapter 13
Ada Wong shows up out of nowhere again, but Leon<lf>wonders where her allegiance truly lies. Is she an ally,<lf>or is she just using him again?<lf>Regardless of Ada's intentions, Leon can now pursue<lf>Krauser and save Ashley thanks to her.
Chapter 14
Leon reunites with Ashley on an isolated island<lf>controlled by the cult, but they're running out of time.<lf>The plaga parasites within them continue to grow<lf>at a horrific rate.
Chapter 15
Although finally able to lay his complicated history with<lf>Krauser to rest, Leon can't afford to waste time being<lf>sentimental now. Saddler has taken control of Ashley<lf>and disappeared into the depths of the island.
Chapter 16
Fighting the parasite for control of his own body, Leon uses<lf>his last remaining strength to get Ashley to the lab in<lf>desperate hope that Luis's legacy can still save them.
Blue Request Notes
The blue papers that you find scattered around the area<lf>are Request Notes. By picking one up, you will accept<lf>a request. The details of accepted requests can be viewed<lf>in the Files menu.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Title_01_0020
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Body_01_0020
Request Rewards
Once you've completed a request, head to the Merchant<lf>to receive spinels as a reward.
Item Crafting
You can create various kinds of ammo by combining<lf>resources and gunpowder. Some knives can also be<lf>used as crafting materials.<lf>Obtaining new crafting recipes will increase the types<lf>of items and ammo that you can create.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Title_01_0040
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Body_01_0040
Managing Items
If your attaché case is full, you can rearrange things in<lf>the Items menu to make room for more items.<lf>Using consumables or crafting items can also create<lf>more space in your inventory.
Knife Attacks
Attacking while your knife is readied will deliver<lf>quick forward thrusts.
Knife Escape
If you have a knife, you will be able to quickly escape<lf>from an enemy in most circumstances.<lf><lf>However, the knife's durability will be greatly reduced.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Title_01_0070
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Body_01_0070
Stealth Kills
If you sneak behind an enemy when you have<lf>a knife, you can take them out in a single move<lf>without making any noise.
Combining Treasures
Some treasures can be sold at a higher price when fitted<lf>with certain gemstones.<lf><lf>View the treasures you've collected in the Key Items &<lf>Treasures menu.
Ashley Commands: Tight Formation
When commanded to move into Tight formation, Ashley<lf>will stick close to Leon at all times.<lf><lf>This formation is particularly useful when on the move<lf>or trying to evade enemies.
Parrying
If you have a knife, some enemy attacks can be<lf>parried by performing the action just before the hit lands.<lf><lf>Time it right and the enemy will be staggered, giving you<lf>a chance to attack.
Ashley Commands: Loose Formation
When commanded to move into Loose formation,<lf>Ashley will hang back and distance herself from Leon.<lf><lf>In this formation, Ashley will protect herself by avoiding<lf>enemies and staying clear of combat.
The Map
The map isn't just for figuring out where you are.<lf>It's also great for seeing where your objectives are<lf>or locating unclaimed items.
Treasure Maps
Treasure maps will point out the locations of<lf>treasure on your map.
Restoring Health
You can restore health using herbs or first aid sprays.<lf>You can also craft more effective recovery items by<lf>combining specific herbs in the Items menu.
Setting Weapon Shortcuts
You can set a weapon to a shortcut by selecting<lf>the weapon in the Items menu.<lf><lf>Up to eight weapons can be assigned at once.
Storage
You can temporarily deposit your equipment via<lf>the Storage menu at any typewriter.<lf><lf>Stash away things like bulky weapons to make<lf>space for other items in your attaché case.
Saving
When you see a typewriter, remember that saving is free,<lf>so save often and save a life.
Used Key Items
Key items that no longer serve a purpose can be sold<lf>to the Merchant.
Melee Attacks
Melee attacks can be used on staggered enemies. If others<lf>are nearby, they will also be knocked back at the same time.<lf><lf>You can then deliver a fatal attack on the struck enemy<lf>with a knife, depending on their position.
Customizing Your Case
You can change your attaché case or swap out charms via<lf>the Customize Case menu at any typewriter.<lf><lf>Cases and charms each have their own special effects.

Quick Turns
You can change the quick turn button or turn the action off<lf>in the Options menu.
When Aiming Weapons
Shooting a weapon while the reticle is zoomed in will<lf>increase the stagger and critical hit rate on enemies.
Crouching
Moving while in the crouched position can help you<lf>avoid enemy detection.
Upgrading Your Weapons
Most weapons can be upgraded by the Merchant.<lf>If you keep running into difficulty during combat,<lf>consider upgrading your weapons to give yourself<lf>some more firepower.
Repairing the Combat Knife
The combat knife can be repaired by the Merchant<lf>if it is broken. It can also be upgraded to increase<lf>its durability, making it harder to break.
Trading
Spinels can be traded in to the Merchant for special items.
Using Typewriters
You can't use typewriters while speaking through comms<lf>or when enemies are nearby.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Title_01_0360
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> CH_Mes_Main_Tips_Body_01_0360
Viewing Information
You can view the contents of documents and comms<lf>that you've received via the Files menu.<lf><lf>They may contain some important information.
Clockwork Castellans
If you ever hear the steady cadence of a wind-up doll,<lf>it means that there's a Clockwork Castellan nearby.<lf><lf>It might be a good idea to find and destroy it.
Scope Magnification
You can choose whether the level of scope<lf>magnification stays the same or resets after<lf>you stop aiming in the Options menu.
Shooting Range
The higher you score, the more tokens you'll earn.<lf>Exchange them at a token machine to receive prizes.
Changing Difficulty
You can change the game's difficulty level from<lf>Standard to Assisted in the game over screen.
Incapacitated Ashley
Ashley will become temporarily incapacitated<lf>if she's attacked.<lf><lf>If attacked again in this state, she will die and<lf>the game will be over.
Captured Ashley
If Ashley is caught by the enemy and carried away,<lf>the game will be over.<lf><lf>Rescue her before the gauge in the bottom-right<lf>corner of the screen runs out.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0012
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Body_02_0012
Parrying
Most enemy attacks can be parried, with some exceptions.<lf>Time a parry just right and the enemy will be staggered,<lf>giving you a chance to follow up with an attack.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0021
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Body_02_0021
Crouch Dodging
Some enemy attacks such as grapples and thrown weapons<lf>can be dodged by crouching.
Knife Kills
You can perform a fatal attack with a knife when you<lf>approach an enemy from behind or stagger them with<lf>something like a flash grenade.
Finishing Enemies Off
Some enemies will get back up even after you think they've<lf>been defeated. You can prevent this by performing a fatal<lf>attack on them with a knife while they are on the ground.
Dynamite
Shooting dynamite will cause it to explode.<lf>This also applies to the unlit sticks of dynamite<lf>held in the hands of certain enemies.
Red-robed Zealots
The chanting prayers of these foes strengthen<lf>other enemies surrounding them.
Throw Attacks
Approach a kneeling enemy from behind to perform<lf>a throw attack.
Plaga Weakness
The parasites that emerge out of the bodies of some<lf>enemies are vulnerable to intense light.<lf><lf>Using weapons that emit light can be very effective.
Knife Defense
Some attacks can be blocked with a knife.
Parasite's Mouth
You can deal a lot of damage to the large parasites<lf>that emerge out of some enemy's bodies by attacking<lf>their weak point—the mouth.
Attacks from Above
Pass below hanging enemies at your own risk.
Latching On
Some parasites can move around independently from the host<lf>and latch on to enemies, making them even more ferocious.<lf>Take them out before they can do this.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0251
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Body_02_0251
The Chainsaw Enemies
The villagers that wield chainsaws are formidable foes.<lf>Don't feel like you have to defeat them; sometimes it's<lf>just better to run away.
Knife Defense
Some attacks can be blocked with a knife.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0042

Sightless Enemies: Sound
Making noise alerts these enemies to your position, so tread<lf>carefully. Walking is quieter than running, and crouching<lf>is quieter than walking.
Sightless Enemies: Weakness
If you attack the exposed parasites on these enemies,<lf>you can cause a lot of damage.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0062
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Body_02_0062
Sightless Enemies: Friendly Fire
These enemies cannot see and are unable to differentiate<lf>between friend and foe. Use this to your advantage by<lf>trying to lure them into the path of another enemy.
Sightless Enemies: Weapons
Enemies that cannot see are more sensitive to sound.<lf>It is wise to use weapons that make less noise when nearby.
Sightless Enemies: Ringing Bells
You can draw the enemy's attention by shooting<lf>a bell to make a loud noise.
Living Armor: Blue Flames
These enemies cannot move when exposed to blue flames.
Living Armor: Armor
You won't get very far attacking the areas protected<lf>by the armor. Instead, aim for the scarcely visible<lf>parasite through the gaps.
Living Armor: Strong Attacks
The two-handed overhead sword attacks are a force to<lf>be reckoned with. Parrying them will greatly reduce<lf>your knife's durability.
Living Armor: Weakness
Exposed parasites are vulnerable to intense light.<lf>Using weapons that emit light can be very effective.
Living Armor: Explosive Weapons
Explosive weapons such as hand grenades are<lf>effective at damaging armored enemies.
Flying Enemies
Flying enemies have the advantage in large, open areas.<lf>Draw them into a confined space to limit their mobility.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0081
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Body_02_0081
Shooting Enemies: Rapid Attacks
Advance against enemies that launch rapid-fire attacks<lf>from a distance by taking cover as you move.
Shooting Enemies: Crossbows
Take advantage of the time it takes for these enemies<lf>to reload. Their magazines explode with light attacks.
<COLOR FF0000>#Rejected#</COLOR> Mes_Main_Tips_Title_02_0092

(“Capcom”), will collect and process your personal data according to our Privacy Policy upon your usage of Resident Evil Village (“Game”). <lf>Privacy Policy (https://www.capcom.co.jp/privacy/game/)<lf><lf>This Game also provides you a function to share your game-play data with the RESIDENT EVIL.NET service (“RE NET”) (https://www.residentevil.net) operated by Capcom. <lf><lf>RE NET is a free interlocking web service support the Resident Evil series, providing features which allows you to view various data such as;<lf>- world statistics based on enormous play data from players all over the world;<lf>- detailed play data; and<lf>- ranking <lf><lf>Your consent to share your gameplay data with the RE NET is optional, and you may freely decide whether to give your consent.  Your gameplay experience will not be affected by the denial of the consent.<lf><lf>Capcom will collect the following personal data with your consent for the following purposes:<lf><lf>Collected information:<lf>(a)  Identifying informationIdentification data provided by the platform providers;<lf>(b)  In-game setting information;<lf>(c)  Gameplay data (including region information); and,<lf>(d)  Logs of in-game communication on the network connection; and,<lf><lf>Purpose of use:<lf>- To enable you to use the services related to this Game on the RE NET website;<lf>- To better understand the Capcom’s users and utilize the findings for product development and marketing purposes of Capcom’s products; and,<lf>- To create statistical data for utilization and publication. <lf><lf><lf>In relation to the RE NET, your personal data will be sent and stored on the server in Japan, managed by Capcom and/or the server in Japan and/or U.S.A of the cloud service providers contracted by Capcom, regardless of your country of residence.<lf>If your data is transferred outside the European Economic Area (EEA) for storage and processing of the data, Capcom will comply with applicable data protection laws, including GDPR.<lf><lf>You may withdraw your consent at any time on “RE NET” from the “Options” screen which will not affect the legitimate process of the data transmitted to Capcom prior to the withdrawal of your consent, and such data will remain accessible on the RE NET website.<lf><lf>Please be noted that, in order to use the RE NET website, you need to consent to the RE NET Terms of Use as well as its Privacy Policy provided separately.  <lf><lf>Do you consent to share your gameplay data with RE NET?<lf><lf>Yes/No

Home Stretch
You rescued Luis, and now he will lead you to the Amber. Follow him.
The Black Robe is a formidable enemy, but many of its attacks can be parried or evaded. Don't take your eyes off it.
You need to escape the castle. Avoid combat as much as possible and take out the enemies quietly.
Once spotted by the enemy, the catapults will start flinging fireballs. If this happens, find a way to destroy them.
It's dangerous up ahead. Avoid combat and find a way to get around the enemy as you continue forward.
Luis didn't show up at the meeting place, but maybe you can find a clue on his location at Méndez's house.
The Black Robe made a sudden appearance. It may grab you if it gets too close, so keep your distance when fighting.
There must be a clue on Luis's whereabouts somewhere. Search every room.
You know where Luis is being held. Check the location of the abandoned factory on your map and make your way there quickly.
If you observe your surroundings closely, you may find Luis's trail.
Many enemies are between you and the villa. It might be a good idea to keep your distance and avoid fighting.
Bullets won't stop Méndez. It's better to use the grapple gun to escape from him.
There's no telling what could be waiting for you in the abandoned factory. Make sure to get ready for a fight before you enter.
The villa where Luis is waiting is not far. However, the route there has changed since last time.
You're vulnerable while on the ground. Get on top of the buildings and aim for the giant's weak points.
In order to suppress the parasite in Ada's body, Luis needs the medicine he developed. Follow him.
Go after Luis in the burning laboratory. He won't last long among the flames.
The locations of the suppressant ingredients are marked on your map. Make sure to read the file titled Suppressant Ingredients too.
The red-robed zealot has stolen the stone that unlocks the door. Track him down and get it.
There's only one ingredient left. Search for the blue butterfly in the collection room accessible from the castle battlements.
Luis has the Amber. Follow his trail and meet up with him.
You can't continue through the waterway without draining the water first. There must be a way to do it.
You can hear the roars of the Black Robe. Prepare for battle before ending things once and for all.
Pesanta has a variety of attacks. Identify the signs of attack, wait for an opening, and prepare to counterattack.
Meet up with Luis and get the Amber.
Krauser has the Amber and you need to go after him. There are some obstacles in your way though, so observe your surroundings and give chase.
Krauser's heading out into the sea. Let's see what his next move is.
A large number of enemies are guarding the way to the comms facility. Reduce their numbers by taking out as many as possible stealthily.
You need to open the shutter to progress. Find something that will open it.
The enemy weapons along the defensive line that guards the comms facility are very powerful. Don't get hit.
You're nearly at the main terminal. Don't worry about the enemies and focus on making your way there.
There's nothing left to do at the comms facility now. Head for the newly opened way out.
The final battle against Saddler lies just up ahead. Take this last opportunity to prepare and upgrade your equipment.
Saddler launches many powerful attacks. Use the terrain to move around and find an opening to perform a counterattack.
The bombs on the island are about to go off. If you don't make it in time, it's over. You better hurry.

Fall, 2004<lf>Ada Wong has infiltrated a menacing castle in rural Europe. Her mission is to retrieve an item of great importance to her client. But when her inside contact gets imprisoned, it's up to Ada to rescue him...before it's too late.
Ada's daring rescue of Luis is cut short by the Black Robe. They are forced to part ways, but not before Luis tells Ada to meet him at the church.<lf><lf>He better have the Amber when she does...
Luis didn't show up at the church...<lf>Ada makes her way to the village chief's manor to look for him but instead encounters Leon, and he's in trouble. Ada saves him, but she needs to keep a low profile for now. Her mission comes first, after all.
While searching for Luis, Ada becomes dizzy before passing out. When she wakes up, she comes face-to-face with Wesker himself, and he isn't pleased. Ada follows his orders and reunites with Luis, but the Amber is still in the castle. The two must venture there again to retrieve it...
Because—you too are infected.<lf>Luis was able to make the suppressant with the ingredients Ada accumulated. He quickly administers it to Ada, but the Black Robe is approaching and the medicine is slow to take effect...
A bad guy...Krauser...Just stole the Amber.<lf>As Ada chases after the man who just killed Luis, she runs into Leon once again. Determined to finish their missions, the two make their way to the island—the cult's stronghold.
Saddler possesses the Amber and Wesker has set his plan to destroy the island in motion. As the bombs count down, Ada returns to pursuing Saddler all the while wondering how this mission will play out.
