Chapter 1
Fall, 2004<lf>Ada Wong has infiltrated a menacing castle in rural Europe.<lf>Her mission is to retrieve an item of great importance to<lf>her client. But when her inside contact gets imprisoned,<lf>it's up to Ada to rescue him...before it's too late.
Chapter 2
Ada's daring rescue of Luis is cut short by the Black Robe.<lf>They are forced to part ways, but not before Luis tells Ada<lf>to meet him at the church.<lf><lf>He better have the Amber when she does...
Chapter 3
Luis didn't show up at the church...<lf>Ada makes her way to the village chief's manor to look<lf>for him but instead encounters Leon, and he's in trouble.<lf>Ada saves him, but she needs to keep a low profile for now.<lf>Her mission comes first, after all.
Chapter 4
While searching for Luis, Ada becomes dizzy before passing<lf>out. When she wakes up, she comes face-to-face with Wesker<lf>himself, and he isn't pleased. Ada follows his orders and<lf>reunites with Luis, but the Amber is still in the castle.<lf>The two must venture there again to retrieve it...
Chapter 5
Because—you too are infected.<lf>Luis was able to make the suppressant with the<lf>ingredients Ada accumulated. He quickly administers<lf>it to Ada, but the Black Robe is approaching and the<lf>medicine is slow to take effect...
Chapter 6
A bad guy...Krauser...Just stole the Amber.<lf>As Ada chases after the man who just killed Luis,<lf>she runs into Leon once again. Determined<lf>to finish their missions, the two make their<lf>way to the island—the cult's stronghold.
Chapter 7
Saddler possesses the Amber and Wesker has set his plan<lf>to destroy the island in motion. As the bombs count down,<lf>Ada returns to pursuing Saddler all the while wondering<lf>how this mission will play out.
The Grapple Gun
The grapple gun allows you to zoom up to advantageous<lf>areas or discover useful items.<lf><lf>Keep a lookout for places where you can use it.
You can attack some staggered enemies from afar by<lf>using the grapple gun to move closer to them.
The I.R.I.S. device equipped in Ada's eye allows her<lf>to see various things almost invisible to the naked eye.<lf><lf>Use it to find clues and complete your mission.
Item Crafting
You can create various kinds of ammo by combining<lf>resources and gunpowder.<lf><lf>Obtaining new crafting recipes will increase the types<lf>of items and ammo that you can create.
Customizing Your Case
You can change your attaché case or swap out charms via<lf>the Customize Case menu at any typewriter.<lf><lf>Cases and charms each have their own special effects.
Repairing the Tactical Knife
Ada's knife can be repaired by the Merchant<lf>if it is broken. It can also be upgraded to increase<lf>its durability, making it harder to break.
Melee Attacks
Melee attacks can be used on staggered enemies. If others<lf>are nearby, they will also be knocked back at the same time.<lf><lf>You can then deliver a fatal attack on the struck enemy<lf>with a knife, depending on their position.
Using Typewriters
You can't use typewriters while speaking through comms<lf>or when enemies are nearby.
Blue Request Notes
The blue papers that you find scattered around the area<lf>are Request Notes. By picking one up, you will accept<lf>a request. The details of accepted requests can be viewed<lf>in the Files menu.
Request Rewards
Once you've completed a request, head to the Merchant<lf>to receive spinels as a reward.
Managing Items
If your attaché case is full, you can rearrange things in<lf>the Items menu to make room for more items.<lf>Using consumables or crafting items can also create<lf>more space in your inventory.
Knife Attacks
Attacking while your knife is readied will deliver<lf>quick forward thrusts.
Knife Escape
If you have a knife, you will be able to quickly escape<lf>from an enemy in most circumstances.<lf><lf>However, the knife's durability will be greatly reduced.
Stealth Kills
If you sneak behind an enemy when you have<lf>a knife, you can take them out in a single move<lf>without making any noise.
Combining Treasures
Some treasures can be sold at a higher price when fitted<lf>with certain gemstones.<lf><lf>View the treasures you've collected in the Key Items &<lf>Treasures menu.
Parrying
If you have a knife, some enemy attacks can be<lf>parried by performing the action just before the hit lands.<lf><lf>Time it right and the enemy will be staggered, giving you<lf>a chance to attack.
The Map
The map isn't just for figuring out where you are.<lf>It's also great for seeing where your objectives are<lf>or locating unclaimed items.
Treasure Maps
Treasure maps will point out the locations of<lf>treasure on your map.
Restoring Health
You can restore health using herbs or first aid sprays.<lf>You can also craft more effective recovery items by<lf>combining specific herbs in the Items menu.
Setting Weapon Shortcuts
You can set a weapon to a shortcut by selecting<lf>the weapon in the Items menu.<lf><lf>Up to eight weapons can be assigned at once.
Storage
You can temporarily deposit your equipment via<lf>the Storage menu at any typewriter.<lf><lf>Stash away things like bulky weapons to make<lf>space for other items in your attaché case.
Saving
When you see a typewriter, remember that saving is free,<lf>so save often and save a life.
Used Key Items
Key items that no longer serve a purpose can be sold<lf>to the Merchant.
Quick Turns
You can change the quick turn button or turn the action off<lf>in the Options menu.
When Aiming Weapons
Shooting a weapon while the reticle is zoomed in will<lf>increase the stagger and critical hit rate on enemies.
Crouching
Moving while in the crouched position can help you<lf>avoid enemy detection.
Upgrading Your Weapons
Most weapons can be upgraded by the Merchant.<lf>If you keep running into difficulty during combat,<lf>consider upgrading your weapons to give yourself<lf>some more firepower.
Trading
Spinels can be traded in to the Merchant for special items.
Viewing Information
You can view the contents of documents and comms<lf>that you've received via the Files menu.<lf><lf>They may contain some important information.
Scope Magnification
You can choose whether the level of scope<lf>magnification stays the same or resets after<lf>you stop aiming in the Options menu.
Changing Difficulty
You can change the game's difficulty level from<lf>Standard to Assisted in the game over screen.
Keep your distance from the Black Robe while attacking.<lf>Its claw attacks can be parried with a knife.
The Black Robe: Phantoms
Hitting the phantom enemies with any attack will cause<lf>them to disappear. Parrying will also have the same effect.
The Black Robe: Real One
The real Black Robe's eyes will shine red just before<lf>it attacks. Keep this in mind as you fight among<lf>all the fake, phantom ones.
The Black Robe: Spear
Try to avoid the Black Robe's sweeping spear attacks with<lf>well-timed evade maneuvers. Thrust attacks can be dodged<lf>by moving out of the way or parrying.
The Black Robe: Close Combat
Stay alert when the Black Robe vanishes; this is a sign<lf>that it is drawing closer to you to launch an attack.<lf>Keep moving to put distance between you and the enemy.
The phantom enemies will disappear when shot, but it's best<lf>to conserve your ammo for when you are fighting the real one.
The Black Robe: Supplies
Keep an eye out for useful items hidden in the fog.
Giant's Weakness
It's hard to aim for the plaga on the giant's back while<lf>on the ground. Zip up to the top of the buildings and<lf>take aim from above the monster instead.
Giant: Timing Your Attacks
It's hard to target the giant's weak point when it's moving<lf>around, but it will be open before and after it attacks.<lf>Take aim during these times.
Giant: Supplies
You can sometimes find useful items among the rubble after<lf>the giant has destroyed a building. Keep a lookout for them<lf>as you dodge the giant's attacks.
The Black Robe's True Form: Tail
Be careful when the monster thrusts its tail into the ground.<lf>An attack is coming, and you should focus on evading it.
The Black Robe's True Form: Projectiles
The fleshy spikes stuck in the ground will cause damage<lf>if you are too close when they burst. Get rid of them with<lf>attacks or wait for them to burst from a safe distance.
The Black Robe's True Form: Movements
Evade the monster when it is frantically moving around<lf>and counterattack when you are at a safe distance.
The Black Robe's True Form: Weaknesses
The monster has weak points on various parts of its body.<lf>Aim for them when the opportunity presents itself.
The Black Robe's True Form: Grenades
Hand grenades are effective when the monster is crawling<lf>around on the ground and covering its weak points.
Saddler: Tentacles
Saddler can use his tentacles to perform wide-ranging<lf>attacks. Don't let your guard down, even if you are far away.
Saddler: Returning Bullets
Saddler can send the bullets you shoot at him back at you.<lf>Get behind some cover when he does.
Saddler: Rush Attacks
If you dodge Saddler's rush attacks by using the grapple<lf>gun, it will give you the opportunity to attack him.
Strong Attacks
Approach a kneeling enemy from behind to perform<lf>a powerful attack.
Countering Catapults
Cannons are effective at taking out catapults.
Being Outnumbered
Don't blindly run into the enemy's defenses.<lf>Carefully observe your surrounds to find useful<lf>things to give you an edge.
Zealots: Crouch Dodging
Some enemy attacks such as grapples can be<lf>dodged by crouching.
Villagers Who Hear the Bell
The villagers will calmly make their way to the church<lf>when the bell is rung—as long as they are not attacked.
Unstable Walkway
If you stop moving, the walkway will collapse and you<lf>will fall to your death. Move quickly and make your<lf>way to a more stable area.
Leaking Steam
Turning the handle will stop steam from leaking out.<lf>Make sure you put distance between yourself and the enemy<lf>so you have enough time to turn it.
Burning Laboratory
Run through the flames and get to Luis before he dies.
Pursuing Drill
Shoot the gongs with the same symbols as the gates<lf>to open them and allow you to escape.
Escaping the Courtyard
You'll need to take the Blue Moonstone from the red-robed<lf>zealot if you want to make your way out of the courtyard.<lf><lf>Pick it up after you defeat him.
Red-robed Zealot: Reinforcements
The longer you leave the red-robed zealot alone,<lf>the more enemy reinforcements will come to his aid.<lf>Take him out first and then deal with the rest.
Hidden Enemies
Keep your eyes peeled for hidden enemies that cling<lf>to the walls. If you spot one, take it out before it stirs.
Underwater Enemies
There are some enemies that lurk in the water,<lf>so keep a lookout for any ripples on the water's surface.
Pounding Rocks
Move under the pounding rocks as they start to rise.<lf>If you time it right, you can also lure pursuing enemies<lf>underneath them as they drop.
Regenerating Enemies: Biosensor Scope
Using a weapon with the biosensor scope mounted onto it<lf>will give you the ability to accurately target the parasites<lf>inside these enemies.<lf><lf>If you don't have one, you can purchase it from the Merchant.
Lift Battle
When you spot an enemy, switch to an appropriate weapon<lf>and take them out quickly before more enemies come.
Lift Battle: Fighting from Afar
Take out enemies from a distance before you get on the lift.<lf>It'll make the battle easier for you.
Pillboxes
Take cover from the pillbox machine guns and try to move<lf>when their laser sights are pointing away from you.
Unknown Test Subject
This enemy won't be affected by any of your attacks.<lf>It's just better to run away.
Slow-moving Lasers
Watch the lasers carefully and look for gaps between<lf>them where you can slip through.
Approaching Lasers
These lasers will kill you instantly when touched.<lf>Stay focused and evade them at all costs.
Rocket Launcher Enemies
The enemies wielding rocket launchers cannot be ignored.<lf>As soon as you see their laser sights, deal with them.
Laser Traps
The laser traps cannot be deactivated, but they can<lf>be destroyed by safely shooting them from a distance.
Countdown to Destruction
You don't have much time before the bombs on the island<lf>start going off. Put all your skills to the test and fight<lf>through the hordes of enemies.

RE NET is a completely free service that gives you a deeper look into the <APP Title_RE_Main2> universe.<lf><lf>Send your play data (game progress and IP address) to gain access to a variety of services,<lf>including a look at your own game, as well as rankings compared to other players.<lf>Play data sent to RE NET may be used for future development.<lf><lf>Would you like to send your play data to RE NET after reading and agreeing to<lf>the terms of service below?<lf><lf>*RE NET settings can be changed at any time from the Options menu.
RE NET is a completely free service that gives you a deeper look into the <APP Title_RE_Main2> universe.<lf><lf>Send your play data (game progress and IP address) to gain access to a variety of services,<lf>including a look at your own game, as well as rankings compared to other players.<lf>Play data sent to RE NET may be used for future development.
Data Processing in BIOHAZARD VILLAGE<lf><lf>We, Capcom Co., Ltd. (“Capcom”), will collect and process your personal data according to our Privacy Policy upon your usage of BIOHAZARD VILLAGE (“Game”). <lf>Privacy Policy (https://www.capcom.co.jp/privacy/game/)<lf><lf>This Game also provides you a function to share your game-play data with the RESIDENT EVIL.NET service (“RE NET”) (https://www.residentevil.net) operated by Capcom. <lf><lf>RE NET is a free interlocking web service support the BIOHAZARD series, providing features which allows you to view various data such as;<lf>- world statistics based on enormous play data from players all over the world;<lf>- detailed play data; and<lf>- ranking <lf><lf>Your consent to share your gameplay data with the RE NET is optional, and you may freely decide whether to give your consent.  Your gameplay experience will not be affected by the denial of the consent.<lf><lf>Capcom will collect the following personal data with your consent for the following purposes:<lf><lf>Collected information:<lf>(a)  Identifying informationIdentification data provided by the platform providers;<lf>(b)  In-game setting information;<lf>(c)  Gameplay data (including region information); and,<lf>(d)  Logs of in-game communication on the network connection; and,<lf><lf>Purpose of use:<lf>- To enable you to use the services related to this Game on the RE NET website;<lf>- To better understand the Capcom’s users and utilize the findings for product development and marketing purposes of Capcom’s products; and,<lf>- To create statistical data for utilization and publication. <lf><lf><lf>In relation to the RE NET, your personal data will be sent and stored on the server in Japan, managed by Capcom and/or the server in Japan and/or U.S.A of the cloud service providers contracted by Capcom, regardless of your country of residence.<lf>If your data is transferred outside the European Economic Area (EEA) for storage and processing of the data, Capcom will comply with applicable data protection laws, including GDPR.<lf><lf>You may withdraw your consent at any time on “RE NET” from the “Options” screen which will not affect the legitimate process of the data transmitted to Capcom prior to the withdrawal of your consent, and such data will remain accessible on the RE NET website.<lf><lf>Please be noted that, in order to use the RE NET website, you need to consent to the RE NET Terms of Use as well as its Privacy Policy provided separately.  <lf><lf>Do you consent to share your gameplay data with RE NET?<lf><lf>Yes/No
